< review>
tandard good thin-crust pizza, I would get it again, but it wouldn't be my first pick. Ordered delivery, a medium create-your-one pizza because we were feeling indecisive. You can choose your own toppings or choose from their menu of specialty pizzas. When you choose your own, they have way more options to choose from than you normally do at other places. You can choose what cheese they use, which sauce, and an array of different toppings. We got pepperoni, arugula, mushrooms, grape tomatoes, and olive oil. It was delivered within 45 minutes. I was pleasantly surprised, but not wowed. It was thin-crust, and a little crispy with each bite. No complaints.</review>

< review>
In 1984, a younger ‚ÄúPapa‚Äù¬†John¬†(Schnatter) transformed a broom closet in his dad's tavern, located in Jeffersonville, Indiana, into a¬†pizza kitchen. He purchase the pizza oven selling his prized, 1971 Camaro Z28.

Fifty years pass so quickly. I'm picking up an order at the Sherman Oaks, independently owned pizzeria that is a Papa John's franchise. The owner, who is also the chef, was knowledgeable and friendly. We bought two large pizzas, one all cheese. And a second, thick crust, vegan pizza, made without cheese. "Papa's" tomato sauce is thick and delicious. The onions, mushrooms and peppers are pilled high, and best of all, both pizzas were cooked perfectly, crisp and well browned.

Everything is wheelchair accessible. Street meter parking is tight. Van Nuys Boulevard is a busy street.  Be careful, exiting your car can be difficult.

Now I've heard of New York Pizza. I've heard of Chicago Pizza. But an Indiana pizza in Los Angeles? Papa would be confused, but proud.< /review>

< review>
Best pizza in WEST HOLLYWOOD! Not only is the pizza great, but the food is authentic Italian cuisine! I found this place while walking my dog, as I passed by the restaurant I smelled the aroma of pizza and I had to turn back around and go inside. First they have hot and ready slices on display, I grabbed 2 slices, I must say it was the best pizza I've had in years. Since I had a big appetite from waking, I decided to try their Steak Entr√©e and Angel Hair pasta! The steak was nice and juicy, fries were crispy, golden & perfectly seasoned. The angel hair was heaven sent , this pasta is worthy of a Michilen Star! Over all, I would definitely eat from here each time I'm in the area. I order here weekly and their service is very prompt! I would recommend this to anyone who is looking for amazing food (with great prices) when in West Hollywood.< /review>

< Review>
Local pizza, pasta, and sub place. They have counter serve, fresh order made, and delivery. The atmosphere is basic and rustic. Indoor and outdoor seating available

Pros:

Quick polite service
Good food at a reasonable price
Wide selection to choose from, including vegetarian and gluten free

Cons:
Counter food sits.... and sits...
The dining room upkeep is meh, finding a clean table even during a slow time can be a challenge

The staff is nice but unmotivated, be patient and willing to ask for things like a clean table, napkins, etc.

Overall an OK place.</Review>

We used to order pizza a lot at work (I suggest the Pesto with Chicken, Sausage, and Mushrooms)  I also LOVE their submarine sandwiches and their greek salad.

When the GIA developed the Four C‚Äôs method of analyzing diamonds, it helped the diamond industry as a whole stabilize and also set certain standards about the quality of a diamond in relation to its price. Now, decades later, jewelers trained by the Gemological Institute of America are qualified to make some quick judgements about a stone‚Äôs quality simply by the price. <pics>None< /pics>< review>
I hate shopping, but I love window shopping! I like going from store to store and thinking about what I'll get some day. And I do usually go back to the stores...someday.

Some stores hate window shoppers...and I get that. You don't make money today off someone looking for a product sometime in the future. Jewelry stores especially seem very touchy about buying something today. I feel a bit claustrophobic when I walk in and the attentive salespeople stare at me the entire time.

This Christmas I took my little brother downtown to buy gifts for people and left him alone for thirty minutes to get me something. What was I to do? Window shop of course! I entered Bert Levi family Jewelers because I am easily attracted to shiny things. They asked me what I wanted of course, and when I responded I was just looking around... they left me alone! It was amazing I didn't buy anything ... but someday I'll want to purchase something shiny...and I'll be sure to keep them in mind.

If you want a low pressure environment I suggest you stop on buy and look at what they have to offer.</review>
